Grand Prix New Jersey 5-0 Trial Decklists
=========================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on October 27, 2018 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/calderaro.jpg)
By Marc Calderaro











With a new Standard format comes my favorite thing of all—new decklists! And to celebrate the best time in the Magic season, here are all the Guilds of Ravnica Standard decklists that earned byes in the Main Event by going undefeated in a Grand Prix Trial. There's tons of archetypes here, and tons of variation even within the archetypes.


Enjoy!








#### Robert Ferguson's Boros Aggro – GP NJ 5-0 Trial


##### 






![Download Arena Decklist](https://web.archive.org/web/20211024134741im_/https://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download_arena.png)
![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
